% 1000-page stress test: random figures of varying widths/heights with lipsum text
% Compiled with LuaLaTeX. Each section has a swarmwrap figure + random lipsum paragraphs.


\section*{Test 1: 4.5cm × 3cm figure}
\begin{multicols}{2}
  \begin{swarmwrap}%
    \begin{minipage}[t]{4cm}
      \centering
      \rule{\linewidth}{3cm}
      \captionof{figure}{Figure 1 in multicol (4cm × 3cm).}
    \end{minipage}%
  \end{swarmwrap}%
  \swarmwrapnext
  \lipsum[72]
  \lipsum[73]
  \lipsum[74]
\end{multicols}
